                        tr:nth-child(even) { background: #f8fafc; }
                        .btn-print { background: #3b82f6; color: white; border: none; padding: 8px 16px; font-weight: bold; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 13px; }
                        .btn-print:hover { background: #2563eb; }
                        @media print {
                            body { padding: 0; }
                            .btn-print { display: none; }
                        }
                    </style>
                </head>
                <body>
                    <div class="header-container">
                        <div>
                            <h1>📊 KRIPTOQUANT Performans Raporu</h1>
                            <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #64748b; margin-top: 4px;">Oluşturulma Tarihi: ${new Date().toLocaleString('tr-TR')}</div>
                        </div>
                        <button class="btn-print" onclick="window.print()">🖨️ Raporu Yazdır / PDF Kaydet</button>
                    </div>

                    <div class="meta-grid">
                        <div class="meta-card">
                            <div class="meta-title">Strateji Bilgileri</div>
                            <div class="meta-value" style="color: #2563eb;">${data.strategyName}</div>
                            <div style="font-size: 12px; margin-top: 6px; color: #475569; line-height: 1.6;">
                                <strong>Coin:</strong> ${data.coin} <br>
                                <strong>Periyot:</strong> ${data.interval} <br>
                                <strong>Dönem:</strong> ${data.startDate} &rarr; ${data.endDate}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="meta-card">
                            <div class="meta-title">Temel Performans Özetleri</div>
                            <div class="meta-value" style="color: ${data.totalReturn >= 0 ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444'};">Getiri: ${data.totalReturn >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${data.totalReturn?.toFixed(2)}%</div>
                            <div style="font-size: 12px; margin-top: 6px; color: #475569; line-height: 1.6;">
                                <strong>Başlangıç / Bitiş Sermayesi:</strong> $${data.initialCapital?.toFixed(2)} &rarr; $${data.finalCapital?.toFixed(2)}<br>
                                <strong>Maks Drawdown:</strong> ${data.maxDrawdown?.toFixed(2)}%<br>
                                <strong>Sharpe Oranı:</strong> ${data.sharpeRatio?.toFixed(2)} | <strong>Sortino:</strong> ${data.sortinoRatio?.toFixed(2)}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <h2>🛠️ Çalıştırılan Test Parametreleri & Risk Kuralları</h2>
                    <table>
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th>Parametre Adı</th>
                                <th>Değer / Ayar</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Stop Loss (Zarar Durdur) Oranı</td>
                                <td style="font-weight: bold;">${slText}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Take Profit (Kar Al) Oranı</td>
                                <td style="font-weight: bold;">${tpText}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Stop Loss ATR Çarpanı</td>
                                <td>${atrMultText}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Maksimum Pozisyon Büyüklüğü (Kasa %)</td>
                                <td>${maxPosText}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Maksimum Emir Büyüklüğü (USDT)</td>
                                <td>${maxOrderText}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Toplam İşlem Sayısı</td>
                                <td>${data.totalTrades} (Kazançlı: ${data.winningTrades} | Kayıplı: ${data.losingTrades} | Başarı Oranı: ${data.winRate?.toFixed(1)}%)</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Profit Factor (Kar Faktörü)</td>
                                <td style="font-weight: bold; color: ${data.profitFactor >= 1.0 ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444'}">${data.profitFactor?.toFixed(2)}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Calmar / MAR Oranı</td>
                                <td>${data.calmarRatio?.toFixed(2)}</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>Time Under Water % (Su Altında Geçen Süre)</td>
                                <td>${data.timeUnderWaterPercent?.toFixed(1)}%</td>
                            </tr>
                            <tr>
                                <td>SQN (System Quality Number)</td>
                                <td>${data.sqn?.toFixed(2) || (data.analytics?.sqn ? data.analytics.sqn.toFixed(2) : '-')}</td>
                            </tr>
                        </tbody>
                    </table>

                    <h2>📋 İşlem Geçmişi Detayları (${trades.length} İşlem)</h2>
                    <table>
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th>Varlık</th>
                                <th>Yön</th>
                                <th>Giriş Zamanı</th>
                                <th>Çıkış Zamanı</th>
                                <th style="text-align: right;">Miktar</th>
                                <th style="text-align: right;">Giriş Fiyatı</th>
                                <th style="text-align: right;">Çıkış Fiyatı</th>
                                <th style="text-align: right;">Net P&L %</th>
                                <th>Çıkış Nedeni</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            ${tradesHtml || '<tr><td colspan="9" style="text-align: center;">Bu testte gerçekleşmiş herhangi bir işlem bulunmamaktadır.</td></tr>'}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </body>
                </html>
            `;

            printWindow.document.write(htmlContent);
            printWindow.document.close();
        }

        // Chart instances cache
        let myEquityChart = null;
        let myMonteCarloChart = null;
        let myRegimeChart = null;
        let myAssetContribChart = null;
        let myYearlyPnlChart = null;

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            loadReportList();
            loadDiscoveryFunnel();
        });

        // ── Tabs Navigation ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
        function switchTab(tabId) {
            const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');
            tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active', 'border-accentBlue', 'text-accentBlue'));
            
            document.getElementById(`tab-${tabId}`).classList.add('active', 'border-accentBlue', 'text-accentBlue');
            
            const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');
            contents.forEach(c => c.classList.add('hidden'));
            
            document.getElementById(`content-${tabId}`).classList.remove('hidden');

            if (tabId === 'compare') {
                renderCompareTab();
            }
        }

        // ── Load list of files from server ──────────────────────────────────
        async function loadReportList() {
            const listEl = document.getElementById('reports-list');
            listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="text-gray-500 text-sm text-center py-8">Raporlar yükleniyor...</div>';
            
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/reports');
                const reports = await res.json();
                
                if (reports.length === 0) {
                    listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="text-gray-500 text-sm text-center py-8">Rapor bulunamadı. Lütfen önce backtest çalıştırın.</div>';
                    return;
                }
                
                // Sort by timestamp desc
                reports.sort((a, b) => b.filename.localeCompare(a.filename));
                
                listEl.innerHTML = '';
                reports.forEach((rep) => {
                    allReportsCache.set(rep.filename, rep);

                    const container = document.createElement('div');
                    container.className = 'w-full p-4 rounded-lg bg-[#111827]/40 hover:bg-[#111827]/80 border border-glassBorder flex items-center justify-between space-x-3 transition-all relative';
                    
                    // Checkbox
                    const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
                    checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
                    checkbox.className = 'w-4 h-4 rounded border-gray-300 text-accentBlue focus:ring-accentBlue z-10 cursor-pointer';
                    checkbox.checked = selectedReports.has(rep.filename);
                    checkbox.onchange = (e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        toggleCompare(rep.filename, checkbox.checked);
                    };

                    // Label/Button
                    const btn = document.createElement('div');
                    btn.className = 'flex-1 cursor-pointer select-none';
                    btn.onclick = () => selectReport(rep.filename, container);

                    const retVal = Number(rep.totalReturn ?? 0);
                    const retStr = retVal >= 0 ? `+${retVal.toFixed(1)}%` : `${retVal.toFixed(1)}%`;
                    const retColor = retVal >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
                    
                    btn.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="flex items-center justify-between w-full">
                            <span class="font-bold text-gray-200 text-xs truncate max-w-[130px]" title="${rep.strategyName}">${rep.strategyName}</span>
                            <span class="text-xs font-semibold ${retColor}">${retStr}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex items-center justify-between w-full mt-2 text-[10px] text-gray-500">
                            <span>${rep.coin.split('+').slice(0, 2).join('+')} | ${rep.interval}</span>
                            <span>Sharpe: ${Number(rep.sharpeRatio ?? 0).toFixed(2)}</span>
                        </div>
                    `;

                    // Delete Button
                    const deleteBtn = document.createElement('button');
                    deleteBtn.className = 'p-1 hover:bg-accentRed/20 text-gray-500 hover:text-accentRed rounded transition-all z-10';
                    deleteBtn.innerHTML = `
                        <svg class="w-3.5 h-3.5" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                            <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M19 7l-.867 12.142A2 2 0 0116.138 21H7.862a2 2 0 01-1.995-1.858L5 7m5 4v6m4-6v6m1-10V4a1 1 0 00-1-1h-4a1 1 0 00-1 1v3M4 7h16" />
                        </svg>
                    `;
                    deleteBtn.onclick = async (e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        if (confirm(`"${rep.filename}" raporunu silmek istediğinize emin misiniz?`)) {
                            try {
                                const res = await fetch(`/api/reports/${encodeURIComponent(rep.filename)}`, {
                                    method: 'DELETE'
                                });
                                const data = await res.json();
                                if (data.success) {
                                    selectedReports.delete(rep.filename);
                                    if (mainReportData && mainReportData.filename === rep.filename) {
                                        mainReportData = null;
                                    }
                                    await loadReportList();
                                } else {
                                    alert('Silme başarısız!');
                                }
                            } catch (err) {
                                alert('Hata: ' + err.message);
                            }
                        }
                    };

                    container.appendChild(checkbox);
                    container.appendChild(btn);
                    container.appendChild(deleteBtn);
                    listEl.appendChild(container);
                });

                // Select first report automatically
                if (reports.length > 0 && !mainReportData) {
                    const firstEl = listEl.querySelector('div');
                    selectReport(reports[0].filename, firstEl);
                }
            } catch (err) {
                listEl.innerHTML = `<div class="text-red-500 text-sm text-center py-8">Yükleme hatası: ${err.message}</div>`;
            }
        }

        function toggleCompare(filename, checked) {
            if (checked) {
                selectedReports.add(filename);
            } else {
                selectedReports.delete(filename);
            }
            document.getElementById('compare-count').innerText = selectedReports.size;
        }

        function clearComparison() {
            selectedReports.clear();
            document.getElementById('compare-count').innerText = 0;
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('#reports-list input[type="checkbox"]');
            checkboxes.forEach(c => c.checked = false);
            renderCompareTab();
        }

        async function selectReport(filename, element) {
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('#reports-list > div');
            cards.forEach(c => c.classList.remove('border-accentBlue', 'bg-[#111827]/80'));
            if (element) {
                element.classList.add('border-accentBlue', 'bg-[#111827]/80');
            }

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/api/reports/${encodeURIComponent(filename)}`);
                const data = await res.json();
                mainReportData = data;
                renderDashboard(data);
            } catch (err) {
                alert('Rapor yüklenemedi: ' + err.message);
            }
        }

        // ── RENDER OVERVIEW DATA ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        function renderDashboard(data) {
            // Set Header Metadata
            document.getElementById('active-strategy-title').innerText = data.strategyName || 'Config-based Strategy';
            document.getElementById('active-coin-subtitle').innerText = `${data.coin} | Interval: ${data.interval}`;
            document.getElementById('active-date-range').innerText = `${data.startDate || ''} → ${data.endDate || ''}`;

            // Decision Outperformance Banner Calculation
            const stratRet = data.totalReturn ?? 0;
            const bhRet = data.buyAndHoldReturn ?? 0;
            const alpha = stratRet - bhRet;

            const decisionBanner = document.getElementById('decision-banner');
            const decisionIcon = document.getElementById('decision-icon');
            const decisionLabel = document.getElementById('decision-label');
            if (alpha > 0) {
                decisionBanner.className = 'p-6 rounded-xl border border-accentGreen/30 bg-accentGreen/5 flex items-center justify-between transition-all';
                decisionIcon.innerHTML = '🥇';
                decisionLabel.innerText = 'OUTPERFORM (Piyasayı Yendi)';
                decisionLabel.className = 'text-xl font-bold mt-0.5 text-accentGreen';
            } else {
                decisionBanner.className = 'p-6 rounded-xl border border-accentRed/30 bg-accentRed/5 flex items-center justify-between transition-all';
                decisionIcon.innerHTML = '⚠️';
                decisionLabel.innerText = 'UNDERPERFORM (Piyasa Gerisinde)';
                decisionLabel.className = 'text-xl font-bold mt-0.5 text-accentRed';
            }

            // AI Recommendation logic
            const sharpe = Number(data.sharpeRatio ?? 0);
            const aiInsightCard = document.getElementById('ai-insight-card');
            const recConfidence = document.getElementById('rec-confidence');
            const recText = document.getElementById('rec-text');
            const recBadge = document.getElementById('rec-badge');
            const recStars = document.getElementById('rec-stars');
            const recAction = document.getElementById('rec-action');
            const whyList = document.getElementById('ai-why-list');

            let confidenceStr = "Düşük (LOW)";
            let badgeText = "❌ AVOID (Uzak Dur)";
            let badgeClass = "text-accentRed";
            let stars = "★★☆☆☆";
            let reasoning = "";
            let actionStr = "Yeniden optimize et";

            if (alpha > 0) {
                if (sharpe >= 3.0) {
                    confidenceStr = "Mükemmel (EXCELLENT)";
                    badgeText = "✅ DEPLOY";
                    badgeClass = "text-accentGreen";
                    stars = "★★★★★";
                    reasoning = `Strateji %${stratRet.toFixed(1)} getiri ile piyasayı (Buy & Hold: %${bhRet.toFixed(1)}) bariz bir şekilde yenmiştir. Sharpe oranı (${sharpe.toFixed(2)}) mükemmel seviyededir. Sistem güvenli limandadır ve kısıt olmaksızın fon yatırımına uygundur.`;
                    actionStr = "Canlı yayına alınabilir";
                } else if (sharpe >= 2.0) {
                    confidenceStr = "İyi (GOOD)";
                    badgeText = "✅ DEPLOY";
                    badgeClass = "text-accentGreen";
                    stars = "★★★★☆";
                    reasoning = `Strateji benchmark'ı geride bırakmış ve %${stratRet.toFixed(1)} net getiri sağlamıştır. Sharpe oranı (${sharpe.toFixed(2)}) tatmin edici düzeydedir. Kontrollü bir şekilde canlı kullanıma alınması önerilir.`;
                    actionStr = "Düşük sermaye ile başlat";
                } else {
                    confidenceStr = "Orta (MODERATE)";
                    badgeText = "⚠️ CAUTION";
                    badgeClass = "text-orange-400";
                    stars = "★★★☆☆";
                    reasoning = `Strateji getiri olarak benchmark'ın üzerinde kalsa da, Sharpe oranı (${sharpe.toFixed(2)}) düşüktür. Bu durum piyasadaki yüksek oynaklık ve volatilite riskini gösterir. Düşük bütçeyle veya korumalı filtrelerle yatırım yapılabilir.`;
                    actionStr = "Trend filtresi ekle";
                }
            } else {
                confidenceStr = "Yüksek (HIGH)";
                badgeText = "❌ AVOID";
                badgeClass = "text-accentRed";
                stars = "★★☆☆☆";
                reasoning = `Strateji getiri olarak pasif piyasa tutma getirisinin (Buy & Hold: %${bhRet.toFixed(1)}) gerisinde kalmıştır. Piyasa performansı stratejiden daha üstün olduğu için bu stratejinin bu haliyle çalıştırılması önerilmez.`;
                actionStr = "Parametreleri sıfırla / optimize et";
            }

            aiInsightCard.className = `glass-card p-6 flex flex-col justify-between lg:col-span-2 border-l-4 ${alpha > 0 ? (sharpe >= 2.0 ? 'border-l-accentGreen' : 'border-l-orange-400') : 'border-l-accentRed'} transition-all`;
            recConfidence.innerText = `Güven Seviyesi: ${confidenceStr}`;
            recText.innerText = reasoning;
            recBadge.innerText = badgeText;
            recBadge.className = `text-sm font-extrabold px-3 py-1 rounded bg-black/20 ${badgeClass}`;
            recStars.innerText = stars;
            recAction.innerText = actionStr;

            // Generate why bullets based on trades
            const trades = data.trades || [];
            const assetPnL = new Map();
            trades.forEach(t => {
                const current = assetPnL.get(t.asset) || 0;
                assetPnL.set(t.asset, current + (t.pnl || 0));
            });

            // Find best and worst assets
            let bestAsset = "";
            let bestPnL = -Infinity;
            let worstAsset = "";
            let worstPnL = Infinity;
            assetPnL.forEach((val, key) => {
                if (val > bestPnL) { bestPnL = val; bestAsset = key; }
                if (val < worstPnL) { worstPnL = val; worstAsset = key; }
            });

            const winRate = Number(data.winRate ?? 0);
            const maxDd = Number(data.maxDrawdown ?? 0);

            let whyHTML = "";
            if (bestAsset && bestPnL > 0) {
                whyHTML += `<li class="flex items-center space-x-2 text-accentGreen"><span>✓</span> <span>${bestAsset} varlığı portföy kârına en yüksek katkıyı sağladı (+${bestPnL.toFixed(0)} USDT).</span></li>`;
            }
            if (worstAsset && worstPnL < 0) {
                whyHTML += `<li class="flex items-center space-x-2 text-accentRed"><span>✗</span> <span>${worstAsset} varlığı net zarar yazarak portföyü aşağı çekti (${worstPnL.toFixed(0)} USDT).</span></li>`;
            }
            if (winRate < 45) {
                whyHTML += `<li class="flex items-center space-x-2 text-accentRed"><span>✗</span> <span>Düşük kazanma oranı (%${winRate.toFixed(1)}): Piyasanın kararsız/yatay olduğu dönemlerde çok sayıda sahte sinyalle (false break) stop olunmuş.</span></li>`;
            } else {
                whyHTML += `<li class="flex items-center space-x-2 text-accentGreen"><span>✓</span> <span>Güçlü kazanma oranı (%${winRate.toFixed(1)}): Trend dönüşleri kararlı bir şekilde yakalanmış.</span></li>`;
            }
            if (maxDd > 20) {
                whyHTML += `<li class="flex items-center space-x-2 text-accentRed"><span>✗</span> <span>Maksimum Çöküş (%${maxDd.toFixed(1)}): Risk toleransı yüksek, kaldıraç veya pozisyon büyüklükleri düşürülmeli.</span></li>`;
            }
            whyList.innerHTML = whyHTML || '<li>Metrikler stabil görünüyor, sıra dışı bir sapma saptanmadı.</li>';

            // Populate Deploy Decision Panel (Problem 8)
            document.getElementById('deploy-badge').innerText = badgeText;
            document.getElementById('deploy-badge').className = `text-2xl font-extrabold block mt-1 tracking-tight ${badgeClass}`;
            document.getElementById('deploy-exp-dd').innerText = `-%${Number(data.maxDrawdown ?? 0).toFixed(1)}`;
            document.getElementById('deploy-exp-cagr').innerText = `%${stratRet.toFixed(1)}`;
            
            const deployScore = Math.round((Math.min(10, Math.max(1, stratRet / 10)) * 0.3 + Math.max(1, Math.min(10, 10 - Number(data.maxDrawdown ?? 0) / 3)) * 0.3 + Math.max(1, Math.min(10, sharpe * 2)) * 0.4) * 10);
            document.getElementById('deploy-confidence').innerText = `%${deployScore}`;
            
            const capRec = alpha > 0 ? Math.min(40, Math.max(5, Math.round(sharpe * 10))) : 0;
            document.getElementById('deploy-cap-rec').innerText = `%${capRec}`;

            // Metrics Cards
            const capPct = `${stratRet >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${stratRet.toFixed(2)}%`;
            document.getElementById('card-capital-pct').innerText = capPct;
            document.getElementById('card-capital-pct').className = `text-3xl font-extrabold ${stratRet >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed'}`;
            document.getElementById('card-capital-val').innerText = `Bitiş: ${(data.finalCapital ?? 0).toLocaleString()} USDT | Başlangıç: ${(data.initialCapital ?? 0).toLocaleString()} USDT`;

            document.getElementById('card-sharpe').innerText = Number(data.sharpeRatio ?? 0).toFixed(3);
            document.getElementById('card-quantscore').innerText = Number(data.quantScore ?? 0).toFixed(4);
            document.getElementById('card-pf').innerText = `Profit Factor: ${Number(data.profitFactor ?? 0).toFixed(3)}`;

            document.getElementById('card-winrate').innerText = `%${winRate.toFixed(1)}`;
            document.getElementById('card-winloss').innerText = `W: ${data.winningTrades ?? 0} | L: ${data.losingTrades ?? 0}`;

            document.getElementById('card-maxdd').innerText = `-%${maxDd.toFixed(2)}`;
            const expectancy = Number(data.analytics?.expectancyUsdt ?? 0);
            document.getElementById('card-avgtrade').innerText = `Expectancy: ${expectancy.toFixed(1)} USDT`;

            // Strategy Scorecard (Problem 4)
            const scoreRetVal = Math.min(10, Math.max(1, Math.round(stratRet / 10)));
            const scoreRiskVal = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, Math.round(10 - maxDd / 3)));
            const scoreRobustVal = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, Math.round(sharpe * 2)));
            const scoreOverfitVal = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, Math.round(10 - sharpe / 1.5)));

            document.getElementById('score-ret').innerText = `${scoreRetVal}/10`;
            document.getElementById('score-risk').innerText = `${scoreRiskVal}/10`;
            document.getElementById('score-robust').innerText = `${scoreRobustVal}/10`;
            document.getElementById('score-overfit').innerText = `${scoreOverfitVal}/10`;
            document.getElementById('score-total').innerText = `${deployScore}/100`;


            calculateAndRenderAssetBreakdown(trades);
            calculateAndRenderYearlyBreakdown(trades);

            // Detailed Risk Tab Metrics
            document.getElementById('risk-rec-factor').innerText = Number(data.analytics?.recoveryFactor ?? 0).toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('risk-mar-ratio').innerText = Number(data.analytics?.marRatio ?? 0).toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('risk-gainpain-ratio').innerText = Number(data.analytics?.gainPainRatio ?? 0).toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('risk-exposure').innerText = `${Number(data.analytics?.exposureTime ?? 0).toFixed(1)}%`;
            document.getElementById('risk-sqn').innerText = Number(data.analytics?.sqn ?? 0).toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('risk-kelly').innerText = `%${(Number(data.analytics?.kelly ?? 0) * 100).toFixed(1)}`;
            document.getElementById('risk-ulcer').innerText = Number(data.analytics?.ulcerIndex ?? 0).toFixed(2);
            document.getElementById('risk-capusage').innerText = `%${(Number(data.analytics?.capitalUsage ?? 0)).toFixed(1)}`;

            const ruinPercent = Number(data.monteCarlo?.riskOfRuinPercent ?? 0);
            document.getElementById('risk-ruin-indicator').innerText = `Risk of Ruin (%30 Limit): %${ruinPercent.toFixed(1)}`;

            // Monte Carlo details
            const mc = data.monteCarlo || {};
            if (mc.finalCapitalQuantiles) {
                document.getElementById('mc-worst').innerText = `${mc.finalCapitalQuantiles.worst?.toLocaleString(undefined, {maximumFractionDigits:0})} $`;
                document.getElementById('mc-p5').innerText = `${mc.finalCapitalQuantiles.p5?.toLocaleString(undefined, {maximumFractionDigits:0})} $`;
                document.getElementById('mc-p50').innerText = `${mc.finalCapitalQuantiles.p50?.toLocaleString(undefined, {maximumFractionDigits:0})} $`;
                document.getElementById('mc-p95').innerText = `${mc.finalCapitalQuantiles.p95?.toLocaleString(undefined, {maximumFractionDigits:0})} $`;
                document.getElementById('mc-best').innerText = `${mc.finalCapitalQuantiles.best?.toLocaleString(undefined, {maximumFractionDigits:0})} $`;
            }

            // Render main Equity chart and Monte Carlo Chart
            renderEquityChart(data.equityCurve || []);
            renderMonteCarloChart(data.monteCarlo || {});
            renderRegimeChart(trades);

            // Populate Trade journal tab
            populateJournalTable(trades);
        }

        // ── CALCULATE ASSET CONTRIBUTION ────────────────────────────────────
        function calculateAndRenderAssetBreakdown(trades) {
            const assetPnL = new Map();
            trades.forEach(t => {
                const current = assetPnL.get(t.asset) || 0;
                assetPnL.set(t.asset, current + (t.pnl || 0));
            });

            const labels = Array.from(assetPnL.keys());
            const data = Array.from(assetPnL.values());
            const colors = data.map(v => v >= 0 ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444');

            const ctx = document.getElementById('assetContribChart').getContext('2d');
            if (myAssetContribChart) myAssetContribChart.destroy();

            myAssetContribChart = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: labels,
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Varlık Net Kârı (USDT)',
                        data: data,
                        backgroundColor: colors,
                        borderRadius: 6
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    scales: {
                        x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#9ca3af' } },
                        y: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' }, ticks: { color: '#9ca3af' } }
                    },
                    plugins: { legend: { display: false } }
                }
            });
        }

        // ── CALCULATE YEARLY P&L ─────────────────────────────────────────────
        function calculateAndRenderYearlyBreakdown(trades) {
            const yearlyPnL = new Map();
            trades.forEach(t => {
                const date = new Date(t.exitOrder.timestamp);
                const year = date.getFullYear();
                if (!isNaN(year)) {
                    const current = yearlyPnL.get(year) || 0;
                    yearlyPnL.set(year, current + (t.pnl || 0));
                }
            });

            const labels = Array.from(yearlyPnL.keys()).sort();
            const data = labels.map(y => yearlyPnL.get(y));
            const colors = data.map(v => v >= 0 ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444');

            const ctx = document.getElementById('yearlyPnlChart').getContext('2d');
            if (myYearlyPnlChart) myYearlyPnlChart.destroy();

            myYearlyPnlChart = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: labels.map(String),
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Yıllık Kar/Zarar (USDT)',
                        data: data,
                        backgroundColor: colors,
                        borderRadius: 6
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    scales: {
                        x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#9ca3af' } },
                        y: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' }, ticks: { color: '#9ca3af' } }
                    },
                    plugins: { legend: { display: false } }
                }
            });
        }

        // ── RENDER MAIN EQUITY & DD CHART ────────────────────────────────────
        function renderEquityChart(curve) {
            const ctx = document.getElementById('equityChartV2').getContext('2d');
            if (myEquityChart) myEquityChart.destroy();

            const labels = curve.map(c => new Date(c.timestamp).toISOString().slice(0, 10));
            const equities = curve.map(c => c.equity);
            const drawdowns = curve.map(c => c.drawdownPercent || 0);

            // Calculate Buy & Hold benchmark line
            const bhRet = Number(mainReportData?.buyAndHoldReturn ?? 0);
            const initialCapital = Number(mainReportData?.initialCapital ?? 10000);
            const bhCurve = curve.map((c, i) => {
                const ratio = i / (curve.length - 1 || 1);
                return initialCapital * (1 + (bhRet / 100) * ratio);
            });

            myEquityChart = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'line',
                data: {
                    labels: labels,
                    datasets: [
                        {
                            label: 'Strateji Sermayesi (USDT)',
                            data: equities,
                            borderColor: '#3b82f6',
                            borderWidth: 2.5,
                            yAxisID: 'y',
                            pointRadius: 0,
                            fill: false
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Buy & Hold Benchmark (USDT)',
                            data: bhCurve,
                            borderColor: '#4b5563',
                            borderWidth: 1.5,
                            borderDash: [5, 5],
                            yAxisID: 'y',
                            pointRadius: 0,
                            fill: false
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Drawdown (%)',
                            data: drawdowns,
                            borderColor: '#ef4444',
                            borderWidth: 1.5,
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.12)',
                            fill: true,
                            yAxisID: 'y1',
                            pointRadius: 0
                        }
                    ]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    scales: {
                        x: {
                            grid: { color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.03)' },
                            ticks: { color: '#9ca3af', maxRotation: 0, font: { size: 10 } }
                        },
                        y: {
                            position: 'left',
                            grid: { color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.04)' },
                            ticks: { color: '#3b82f6' }
                        },
                        y1: {
                            position: 'right',
                            grid: { display: false },
                            ticks: { color: '#ef4444' },
                            reverse: true,
                            min: 0,
                            max: 100
                        }
                    },
                    plugins: {
                        legend: { labels: { color: '#f1f5f9' } }
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // ── RENDER MONTE CARLO CHART ─────────────────────────────────────────
        function renderMonteCarloChart(mc) {
            const ctx = document.getElementById('monteCarloChartV2').getContext('2d');
            if (myMonteCarloChart) myMonteCarloChart.destroy();

            if (!mc || !mc.finalCapitalQuantiles) return;

            const q = mc.finalCapitalQuantiles;
            const labels = ['Worst Path', 'P5 (Kötü %5)', 'P50 (Ortanca)', 'P95 (İyi %5)', 'Best Path'];
            const data = [q.worst, q.p5, q.p50, q.p95, q.best];

            myMonteCarloChart = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: labels,
                    datasets: [{
                        data: data,
                        backgroundColor: ['#ef4444', '#f97316', '#3b82f6', '#10b981', '#059669'],
                        borderRadius: 8
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    scales: {
                        x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#9ca3af' } },
                        y: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.04)' }, ticks: { color: '#9ca3af' } }
                    },
                    plugins: { legend: { display: false } }
                }
            });
        }

        // ── RENDER REGIME doughnut CHART ──────────────────────────────────────
        function renderRegimeChart(trades) {
            const ctx = document.getElementById('riskRegimeChart').getContext('2d');
            if (myRegimeChart) myRegimeChart.destroy();

            let wins = 0;
            let losses = 0;
            trades.forEach(t => {
                if (t.pnlPercent >= 0) wins++;
                else losses++;
            });

            myRegimeChart = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'doughnut',
                data: {
                    labels: ['Karlı İşlemler', 'Zararlı İşlemler'],
                    datasets: [{
                        data: [wins, losses],
                        backgroundColor: ['#10b981', '#ef4444'],
                        borderWidth: 0
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: { position: 'bottom', labels: { color: '#9ca3af' } }
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // ── RENDER COMPARE MODULE (Sekme 3) ──────────────────────────────────
        async function renderCompareTab() {
            const tableBody = document.getElementById('compare-table-body');
            const tableHeader = document.querySelector('#compare-table thead tr');
            
            if (selectedReports.size === 0) {
                tableBody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="10" class="py-8 text-center text-gray-500">Lütfen karşılaştırmak için soldaki listeden en az iki kutucuğu işaretleyin.</td></tr>';
                document.getElementById('badge-winner').innerText = '🥇 Seçim Yapılmadı';
                return;
            }

            // Fetch all reports contents in parallel
            const reportDataList = [];
            for (const filename of selectedReports) {
                try {
                    const res = await fetch(`/api/reports/${encodeURIComponent(filename)}`);
                    const data = await res.json();
                    reportDataList.push(data);
                } catch {}
            }

            // Render Headers
            tableHeader.innerHTML = '<th class="pb-4 font-semibold">Metrik / Özellik</th>';
            reportDataList.forEach(data => {
                tableHeader.innerHTML += `<th class="pb-4 font-semibold text-center">${data.strategyName || 'Strategy'}</th>`;
            });

            // Compare Rows config
            const rowsConfig = [
                { label: 'Coin / Varlık', key: 'coin', type: 'string' },
                { label: 'Mum Aralığı', key: 'interval', type: 'string' },
                { label: 'Strateji Getirisi (%)', key: 'totalReturn', type: 'pct', higherBetter: true },
                { label: 'Buy & Hold Getirisi (%)', key: 'buyAndHoldReturn', type: 'pct', higherBetter: true },
                { label: 'Sharpe Oranı', key: 'sharpeRatio', type: 'num', higherBetter: true },
                { label: 'Maksimum Çöküş (%)', key: 'maxDrawdown', type: 'dd', higherBetter: false },
                { label: 'Kazanma Oranı (%)', key: 'winRate', type: 'pct', higherBetter: true },
                { label: 'Profit Factor', key: 'profitFactor', type: 'num', higherBetter: true },
                { label: 'Toplam İşlem Sayısı', key: 'totalTrades', type: 'int', higherBetter: true },
            ];

            // Build Rows HTML
            tableBody.innerHTML = '';
            rowsConfig.forEach(row => {
                let html = `<tr class="hover:bg-slate-800/20"><td class="py-3.5 font-medium text-gray-400">${row.label}</td>`;
                
                // Find best value index to highlight it
                let bestIdx = -1;
                if (row.type !== 'string') {
                    let bestVal = row.higherBetter ? -Infinity : Infinity;
                    reportDataList.forEach((data, idx) => {
                        const val = data[row.key] ?? 0;
                        if (row.higherBetter) {
                            if (val > bestVal) { bestVal = val; bestIdx = idx; }
                        } else {
                            if (val < bestVal) { bestVal = val; bestIdx = idx; }
                        }
                    });
                }

                reportDataList.forEach((data, idx) => {
                    let val = data[row.key];
                    let text = val;
                    if (row.type === 'pct') text = `%${val?.toFixed(2)}`;
                    else if (row.type === 'dd') text = `-%${val?.toFixed(2)}`;
                    else if (row.type === 'num') text = val?.toFixed(3);
                    else if (row.type === 'int') text = val?.toString();

                    const highlightClass = idx === bestIdx ? 'text-accentGreen font-bold bg-accentGreen/5' : 'text-gray-200';
                    html += `<td class="py-3.5 text-center font-mono ${highlightClass}">${text}</td>`;
                });
                html += '</tr>';
                tableBody.innerHTML += html;
            });

            // Find overall winner based on Sharpe Ratio
            let bestSharpe = -Infinity;
            let winnerName = 'Bulunamadı';
            reportDataList.forEach(data => {
                if ((data.sharpeRatio ?? 0) > bestSharpe) {
                    bestSharpe = data.sharpeRatio ?? 0;
                    winnerName = data.strategyName;
                }
            });
            document.getElementById('badge-winner').innerText = `🥇 Öneri: ${winnerName} (Yüksek Sharpe)`;
        }

        // ── POPULATE JOURNAL TABLE (Sekme 4) ──────────────────────────────────
        let allTradesCache = [];
        function populateJournalTable(trades) {
            allTradesCache = trades;
            filterTradesTable();
        }

        function filterTradesTable() {
            const query = document.getElementById('journal-search').value.toLowerCase();
            const tbody = document.getElementById('journal-table-body');
            tbody.innerHTML = '';

            const filtered = allTradesCache.filter(t => {
                const asset = (t.asset || t.coin || '').toLowerCase();
                const reason = (t.exitReason || '').toLowerCase();
                return asset.includes(query) || reason.includes(query);
            });

            document.getElementById('journal-trades-subtitle').innerText = `${filtered.length} işlem filtrelendi (Toplam: ${allTradesCache.length})`;

            filtered.forEach(t => {
                const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                tr.className = 'hover:bg-slate-800/30 transition-all';
                
                const asset = t.asset || t.coin || 'USDT';
                const side = (t.entryOrder && t.entryOrder.side) || t.side || 'BUY';
                const qty = (t.entryOrder && t.entryOrder.quantity) || t.quantity || 1.0;
                const entryPrice = (t.entryOrder && t.entryOrder.price) || t.entryPrice || 0.0;
                const exitPrice = (t.exitOrder && t.exitOrder.price) || t.exitPrice || 0.0;
                const pnlPct = typeof t.pnlPercent === 'number' ? t.pnlPercent : (t.realizedPnLPercent || 0.0);
                const exitReason = t.exitReason || '';
                const entryTime = t.entryOrder ? formatDateTime(t.entryOrder.timestamp) : '-';
                const exitTime = t.exitOrder ? formatDateTime(t.exitOrder.timestamp) : '-';

                const sideColor = side === 'BUY' ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
                const pnlColor = pnlPct >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
                
                tr.innerHTML = `
                    <td class="py-3 font-semibold text-gray-200">${asset}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 font-bold ${sideColor}">${side}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400 font-mono">${entryTime}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400 font-mono">${exitTime}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">${qty.toFixed(4)}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">${entryPrice.toFixed(2)}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">${exitPrice.toFixed(2)}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-right font-bold font-mono ${pnlColor}">${pnlPct >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${pnlPct.toFixed(2)}%</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400 max-w-[150px] truncate" title="${exitReason}">${exitReason}</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-right text-accentRed font-mono">${(t.mae ?? 0).toFixed(2)}%</td>
                    <td class="py-3 text-right text-accentGreen font-mono">${(t.mfe ?? 0).toFixed(2)}%</td>
                `;
                tbody.appendChild(tr);
            });
        }

        async function runCustomBacktest() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('btn-run-backtest');
            if (!btn) return;
            const originalHTML = btn.innerHTML;
            
            const strategyType = document.getElementById('builder-type').value;
            const customName = document.getElementById('builder-name')?.value.trim() || 'my-custom-strategy';
            const coin = document.getElementById('builder-run-coin').value.trim();
            const interval = document.getElementById('builder-run-interval').value;
            
            const slVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-sl').value);
            const sl = !isNaN(slVal) ? slVal : 2.5;
            const tpVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-tp').value);
            const tp = !isNaN(tpVal) ? tpVal : 6.0;
            
            const startDate = document.getElementById('builder-start-date').value;
            const endDate = document.getElementById('builder-end-date').value;
            
            const riskAllocation = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-risk-allocation').value) || 20;
            const riskMaxOrder = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-risk-max-order').value) || 2000;
            const atrVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-risk-atr-mult').value);
            const riskAtrMult = !isNaN(atrVal) ? atrVal : 2.0;
            const disableFilters = document.getElementById('builder-disable-filters')?.checked || false;

            let fastPeriod = 9;
            let slowPeriod = 21;
            let donchianPeriod = 20;
            let vwapPeriod = 20;
            let vwapThreshold = 2.0;
            let bollingerPeriod = 20;
            let bollingerMultiplier = 2.0;
            
            const fastEl = document.getElementById('builder-ema-fast') || document.getElementById('builder-sma-fast');
            if (fastEl) fastPeriod = parseInt(fastEl.value);
            
            const slowEl = document.getElementById('builder-ema-slow') || document.getElementById('builder-sma-slow');
            if (slowEl) slowPeriod = parseInt(slowEl.value);
            
            const donchianEl = document.getElementById('builder-donchian-period');
            if (donchianEl) donchianPeriod = parseInt(donchianEl.value);

            const vwapPeriodEl = document.getElementById('builder-vwap-period');
            if (vwapPeriodEl) vwapPeriod = parseInt(vwapPeriodEl.value);

            const vwapThresholdEl = document.getElementById('builder-vwap-threshold');
            if (vwapThresholdEl) vwapThreshold = parseFloat(vwapThresholdEl.value);

            const bollingerPeriodEl = document.getElementById('builder-bollinger-period');
            if (bollingerPeriodEl) bollingerPeriod = parseInt(bollingerPeriodEl.value);

            const bollingerMultiplierEl = document.getElementById('builder-bollinger-mult');
            if (bollingerMultiplierEl) bollingerMultiplier = parseFloat(bollingerMultiplierEl.value);

            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.innerHTML = '<span>⏳ Backtest Koşuyor, Lütfen Bekleyin...</span>';
            
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/backtest/run', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        strategy: strategyType,
                        customName: customName,
                        coin: coin,
                        interval: interval,
                        fastPeriod,
                        slowPeriod,
                        donchianPeriod,
                        vwapPeriod,
                        vwapThreshold,
                        bollingerPeriod,
                        bollingerMultiplier,
                        stopLossPercent: sl / 100,
                        takeProfitPercent: tp / 100,
                        startDate,
                        endDate,
                        maxPositionPercent: riskAllocation,
                        maxOrderValue: riskMaxOrder,
                        stopLossAtrMultiplier: riskAtrMult,
                        disableFilters: disableFilters
                    })
                });
                
                const data = await res.json();
                if (data.success) {
                    alert('Backtest başarıyla tamamlandı!');
                    // Refresh reports list
                    await loadReportList();
                    // Load the newly generated report if we can find it
                    if (data.filename) {
                        selectReport(data.filename);
                    }
                } else {
                    alert('Backtest hatası: ' + (data.error || 'Bilinmeyen hata'));
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
                alert('Sunucu hatası oluştu!');
            } finally {
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
            }
        }

        // ── LOAD DISCOVERY FUNNEL (Sekme 5) ──────────────────────────────────
        async function loadDiscoveryFunnel() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/discovery');
                const data = await res.json();

                if (!data.results || data.results.length === 0) return;

                // Simple stage count calculations based on discovery log results
                const total = data.totalCandidates || 50;
                
                // Count passes per stage
                let btCount = 0;
                let mcCount = 0;
                let wfCount = 0;

                data.results.forEach(r => {
                    // Passed backtest stage means stage is at least not BACKTEST_FAILED or INSUFFICIENT_TRADES
                    if (r.stage !== 'BACKTEST_FAILED' && r.stage !== 'INSUFFICIENT_TRADES') btCount++;
                    if (r.stage !== 'BACKTEST_FAILED' && r.stage !== 'INSUFFICIENT_TRADES' && r.stage !== 'MONTE_CARLO_FAILED') mcCount++;
                    if (r.stage === 'PASSED') wfCount++;
                });

                // Update funnel width sizes
                document.getElementById('funnel-total').style.width = '100%';
                document.getElementById('funnel-total').innerText = `${total} Aday Arama`;

                const btPct = total > 0 ? (btCount / total * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;
                document.getElementById('funnel-bt').style.width = `${btPct}%`;
                document.getElementById('funnel-bt').innerText = `${btCount} Aday (Kârlı Backtest) | %${btPct}`;

                const mcPct = btCount > 0 ? (mcCount / total * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;
                document.getElementById('funnel-mc').style.width = `${mcPct}%`;
                document.getElementById('funnel-mc').innerText = `${mcCount} Aday (Monte Carlo Güvenli) | %${mcPct}`;

                const wfPct = mcCount > 0 ? (wfCount / total * 100).toFixed(0) : 0;
                document.getElementById('funnel-wf').style.width = `${wfPct}%`;
                document.getElementById('funnel-wf').innerText = `${wfCount} Aday (Walk-Forward Robust) | %${wfPct}`;

                // Discovery Leaderboard
                const sorted = data.results.filter(r => r.stage === 'PASSED')
                    .sort((a,b) => (b.score?.overall ?? 0) - (a.score?.overall ?? 0))
                    .slice(0, 10);

                const leaderboardEl = document.getElementById('discovery-leaderboard');
                if (sorted.length === 0) {
                    leaderboardEl.innerHTML = '<div class="text-gray-500 text-xs text-center py-8">Walk-Forward aşamasını geçen aday bulunamadı.</div>';
                    return;
                }

                leaderboardEl.innerHTML = '';
                sorted.forEach((item, idx) => {
                    const stars = '★'.repeat(Math.min(5, Math.ceil((item.score?.overall ?? 0) / 20)));
                    
                    // Check if we can find a matching filename in cache
                    let filename = "";
                    for (const key of allReportsCache.keys()) {
                        if (key.includes(item.id) || key.includes(item.strategyName)) {
                            filename = key;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    const card = document.createElement('div');
                    card.className = 'p-3 bg-black/30 border border-glassBorder rounded-lg flex items-center justify-between text-xs transition-all ' + (filename ? 'cursor-pointer hover:border-accentBlue hover:bg-black/50' : '');
                    if (filename) {
                        card.onclick = () => {
                            switchTab('overview');
                            selectReport(filename);
                        };
                        card.title = "Ayrıntılı Raporu Yükle";
                    }

                    card.innerHTML = '<div>' +
                        '<span class="font-bold text-gray-200 block">' + (idx === 0 ? '🥇' : idx === 1 ? '🥈' : idx === 2 ? '🥉' : '#' + (idx + 1)) + ' ' + item.id + '</span>' +
                        '<span class="text-gray-500 mt-1 block">Sharpe: ' + Number(item.sharpeRatio ?? 0).toFixed(2) + ' | DD: -%' + Number(item.maxDrawdown ?? 0).toFixed(1) + '</span>' +
                        '</div>' +
                        '<div class="text-right">' +
                        '<span class="text-accentGreen font-bold block">+' + Number(item.totalReturn ?? 0).toFixed(1) + '%</span>' +
                        '<span class="text-yellow-500 font-mono mt-1 block">' + stars + '</span>' +
                        '</div>';
                    leaderboardEl.appendChild(card);
                });

            } catch (err) {}
        }

        // ── DSL BUILDER JS LOGIC ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        function toggleBuilderFields() {
            const type = document.getElementById('builder-type').value;
            const fieldsEl = document.getElementById('builder-fields');
            
            if (type === 'ema-cross') {
                fieldsEl.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Hızlı EMA Periyodu</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-ema-fast" oninput="generateDSL()" value="9" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Yavaş EMA Periyodu</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-ema-slow" oninput="generateDSL()" value="21" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            } else if (type === 'donchian') {
                fieldsEl.innerHTML = `
                    <div>
                        <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Kanal Periyodu (Period)</label>
                        <input type="number" id="builder-donchian-period" oninput="generateDSL()" value="20" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                    </div>
                `;
            } else if (type === 'supertrend') {
                fieldsEl.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">ATR Periyodu</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-st-period" oninput="generateDSL()" value="10" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Çarpan (Multiplier)</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-st-mult" oninput="generateDSL()" value="3.0" step="0.1" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            } else if (type === 'vwap-zscore') {
                fieldsEl.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">VWAP Periyodu</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-vwap-period" oninput="generateDSL()" value="20" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Z-Score Eşik (Threshold)</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-vwap-threshold" oninput="generateDSL()" value="2.0" step="0.1" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            } else if (type === 'bollinger-bands') {
                fieldsEl.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Bant Periyodu</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-bollinger-period" oninput="generateDSL()" value="20" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                        <div>
                            <label class="block text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-semibold mb-1 uppercase font-mono">Standart Sapma Çarpanı</label>
                            <input type="number" id="builder-bollinger-mult" oninput="generateDSL()" value="2.0" step="0.1" class="w-full bg-[#090d16] border border-glassBorder px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-gray-200">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }

        function generateDSL() {
            const name = document.getElementById('builder-name').value;
            const type = document.getElementById('builder-type').value;
            const sl = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-sl').value);
            const tp = parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-tp').value);
            
            let params = {};
            if (type === 'ema-cross') {
                params = {
                    fastPeriod: parseInt(document.getElementById('builder-ema-fast')?.value || 9),
                    slowPeriod: parseInt(document.getElementById('builder-ema-slow')?.value || 21)
                };
            } else if (type === 'donchian') {
                params = {
                    period: parseInt(document.getElementById('builder-donchian-period')?.value || 20)
                };
            } else if (type === 'supertrend') {
                params = {
                    period: parseInt(document.getElementById('builder-st-period')?.value || 10),
                    multiplier: parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-st-mult')?.value || 3.0)
                };
            } else if (type === 'vwap-zscore') {
                params = {
                    vwapPeriod: parseInt(document.getElementById('builder-vwap-period')?.value || 20),
                    vwapThreshold: parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-vwap-threshold')?.value || 2.0)
                };
            } else if (type === 'bollinger-bands') {
                params = {
                    bollingerPeriod: parseInt(document.getElementById('builder-bollinger-period')?.value || 20),
                    bollingerMultiplier: parseFloat(document.getElementById('builder-bollinger-mult')?.value || 2.0)
                };
            }

            const config = {
                name: name,
                indicator: type,
                params: params,
                risk: {
                    stopLossPercent: sl,
                    takeProfitPercent: tp
                }
            };

            document.getElementById('builder-output').value = JSON.stringify(config, null, 4);
        }

        function copyDSLJson() {
            const output = document.getElementById('builder-output');
            output.select();
            document.execCommand('copy');
            alert('Strateji JSON yapılandırması panoya kopyalandı!');
        }

        // ── LIVE PAPER TRADING JS LOGIC ──────────────────────────────────────────
        let liveSocket = null;

        function connectLiveWebSocket() {
            const proto = location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss' : 'ws';
            const wsUrl = proto + '://' + location.host + '/ws/live';
            console.log("Connecting to Live Event Bus WS...", wsUrl);
            
            liveSocket = new WebSocket(wsUrl);

            liveSocket.onmessage = (event) => {
                try {
                    const state = JSON.parse(event.data);
                    renderLiveState(state);
                } catch (e) {
                    console.error("Failed to parse live state message:", e);
                }
            };

            liveSocket.onclose = () => {
                console.log("Live WS closed. Reconnecting in 3s...");
                setTimeout(connectLiveWebSocket, 3000);
            };
        }

        async function deployPaperEngine() {
            const strategy = document.getElementById('live-strategy-select').value;
            const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="live-coin"]:checked');
            const coins = Array.from(checkboxes).map(cb => cb.value);
            
            if (coins.length === 0) {
                alert('Lütfen en az bir coin / varlık seçin.');
                return;
            }
            
            const interval = document.getElementById('live-interval-select').value;

            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/live-paper/start', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ strategy, coins, interval })
                });
                const data = await res.json();
                if (data.success) {
                    alert('Live Paper Trading Engine başarıyla başlatıldı!');
                } else {
                    alert('Hata: ' + data.message);
                }
            } catch (e) {
                alert('Motor başlatılamadı: ' + e.message);
            }
        }

        async function stopPaperEngine() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/live-paper/stop', { method: 'POST' });
                const data = await res.json();
                if (data.success) {
                    alert('Live Paper Trading Engine durduruldu.');
                } else {
                    alert('Hata: ' + data.message);
                }
            } catch (e) {
                alert('Motor durdurulamadı: ' + e.message);
            }
        }

        function renderLiveState(state) {
            // 1) Status Badge & Uptime & heartbeat
            const badge = document.getElementById('live-status-badge');
            const btnDeploy = document.getElementById('btn-deploy-paper');
            const btnStop = document.getElementById('btn-stop-paper');

            if (state.engineStatus === 'running') {
                badge.innerText = 'CANLI ÇALIŞIYOR';
                badge.className = 'px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-bold uppercase bg-accentGreen/20 text-accentGreen animate-pulse';
                btnDeploy.disabled = true;
                btnDeploy.className = 'px-5 py-2.5 bg-accentGreen/20 text-gray-500 font-bold text-xs rounded-lg cursor-not-allowed';
                btnStop.disabled = false;
                btnStop.className = 'px-5 py-2.5 bg-accentRed hover:bg-accentRed/80 text-white font-bold text-xs rounded-lg transition-all';
                
                // Blink heartbeat green
                document.getElementById('live-heartbeat-dot').className = 'w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-accentGreen animate-ping';
            } else {
                badge.innerText = 'DURDURULDU';
                badge.className = 'px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-bold uppercase bg-gray-800 text-gray-400';
                btnDeploy.disabled = false;
                btnDeploy.className = 'px-5 py-2.5 bg-accentGreen hover:bg-accentGreen/80 text-black font-bold text-xs rounded-lg transition-all';
                btnStop.disabled = true;
                btnStop.className = 'px-5 py-2.5 bg-accentRed/20 text-gray-500 font-bold text-xs rounded-lg cursor-not-allowed';
                
                document.getElementById('live-heartbeat-dot').className = 'w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-gray-500';
            }

            // Format uptime
            const u = state.uptime || 0;
            const hrs = String(Math.floor(u / 3600)).padStart(2, '0');
            const mins = String(Math.floor((u % 3600) / 60)).padStart(2, '0');
            const secs = String(u % 60).padStart(2, '0');
            document.getElementById('live-uptime-val').innerText = hrs + ':' + mins + ':' + secs;
            document.getElementById('live-lastcandle-val').innerText = state.lastCandleTime ? new Date(state.lastCandleTime).toLocaleTimeString() : '--:--:--';
            document.getElementById('live-heartbeat-val').innerText = state.heartbeat ? new Date(state.heartbeat).toLocaleTimeString() : '--';

            // 2) Account info
            document.getElementById('live-equity-val').innerText = '$' + (state.currentEquity ?? 10000).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
            document.getElementById('live-cash-val').innerText = '$' + (state.cash ?? 10000).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
            
            const realizedColor = (state.realizedPnL ?? 0) >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
            document.getElementById('live-realized-val').innerText = '$' + (state.realizedPnL ?? 0).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
            document.getElementById('live-realized-val').className = 'text-base font-bold ' + realizedColor;

            const unrealizedColor = (state.unrealizedPnL ?? 0) >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
            document.getElementById('live-unrealized-val').innerText = '$' + (state.unrealizedPnL ?? 0).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
            document.getElementById('live-unrealized-val').className = 'text-base font-bold ' + unrealizedColor;
            document.getElementById('live-trades-count').innerText = state.closedTrades ? state.closedTrades.length : 0;

            // 3) Active positions table
            const posBody = document.getElementById('live-positions-body');
            posBody.innerHTML = '';
            if (!state.activePositions || state.activePositions.length === 0) {
                posBody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="10" class="py-6 text-center text-gray-500">Açık pozisyon bulunmuyor.</td></tr>';
            } else {
                state.activePositions.forEach(p => {
                    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                    tr.className = 'hover:bg-slate-800/30 transition-all font-mono';
                    
                    const pnlColor = p.currentPnLPercent >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen font-bold' : 'text-accentRed font-bold';
                    const sign = p.currentPnLPercent >= 0 ? '+' : '';
                    
                    tr.innerHTML = '<td>' + p.coin + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-gray-400 font-sans">' + p.strategyName + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-300 font-mono">' + p.entryPrice.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-300 font-mono">' + p.currentPrice.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">' + p.quantity.toFixed(4) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-accentRed font-mono">' + p.stopLoss.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-accentGreen font-mono">' + p.takeProfit.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">' + (p.mae ?? 0).toFixed(2) + '%</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">' + (p.mfe ?? 0).toFixed(2) + '%</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right font-bold font-mono ' + pnlColor + '">' + sign + p.currentPnLPercent.toFixed(2) + '% ($' + sign + p.currentPnLUsdt.toFixed(2) + ')</td>';
                    posBody.appendChild(tr);
                });
            }

            // 4) Signals watch list
            const signalList = document.getElementById('live-signals-list');
            signalList.innerHTML = '';
            if (!state.pendingSignals || state.pendingSignals.length === 0) {
                signalList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-gray-500 text-xs text-center py-8">Henüz üretilmiş bir sinyal bulunmuyor.</div>';
            } else {
                const reversedSignals = [...state.pendingSignals].reverse();
                reversedSignals.forEach(s => {
                    const sideColor = s.side === 'BUY' ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
                    const badge = document.createElement('div');
                    badge.className = 'p-2.5 bg-black/30 border border-glassBorder rounded-lg flex items-center justify-between text-xs font-mono';
                    badge.innerHTML = '<div class="flex items-center space-x-2">' +
                            '<span class="font-bold text-gray-200">' + s.coin + '</span>' +
                            '<span class="text-gray-500">|</span>' +
                            '<span class="text-gray-400">' + new Date(s.time).toLocaleTimeString() + '</span>' +
                        '</div>' +
                        '<div class="flex items-center space-x-2">' +
                            '<span class="' + sideColor + ' font-bold">' + s.side + '</span>' +
                            '<span class="text-gray-500">@</span>' +
                            '<span class="text-gray-200">' + s.price.toFixed(2) + '</span>' +
                        '</div>';
                    signalList.appendChild(badge);
                });
            }

            // 5) Live Trade journal
            const journalBody = document.getElementById('live-journal-body');
            journalBody.innerHTML = '';
            if (!state.closedTrades || state.closedTrades.length === 0) {
                journalBody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="9" class="py-6 text-center text-gray-500">Tamamlanmış işlem bulunmuyor.</td></tr>';
            } else {
                const reversedTrades = [...state.closedTrades].reverse();
                reversedTrades.forEach(t => {
                    const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                    tr.className = 'hover:bg-slate-800/30 transition-all font-mono';
                    
                    const pnlColor = t.realizedPnLPercent >= 0 ? 'text-accentGreen' : 'text-accentRed';
                    const sign = t.realizedPnLPercent >= 0 ? '+' : '';
                    
                    const dur = t.holdingDurationSeconds || 0;
                    let durStr = dur + 's';
                    if (dur > 60) {
                        durStr = Math.floor(dur / 60) + 'dk ' + (dur % 60) + 's';
                    }
                    
                    tr.innerHTML = '<td class="py-3 font-semibold text-gray-200">' + t.coin + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-gray-400 font-mono">' + t.entryPrice.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-gray-400 font-mono">' + t.exitPrice.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 font-bold font-mono ' + pnlColor + '">' + sign + t.realizedPnLPercent.toFixed(2) + '% ($' + sign + t.realizedPnLUsdt.toFixed(2) + ')</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-gray-400 max-w-[120px] truncate" title="' + t.exitReason + '">' + t.exitReason + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-gray-400 font-mono">' + durStr + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-accentRed font-mono">' + (t.mae ?? 0).toFixed(2) + '%</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right text-accentGreen font-mono">' + (t.mfe ?? 0).toFixed(2) + '%</td>' +
                        '<td class="py-3 text-right font-bold text-gray-200 font-mono">' + (t.rMultiple ?? 0).toFixed(2) + 'R</td>';
                    journalBody.appendChild(tr);
                });
            }
        }

        // Initialize Builder dynamically
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            toggleBuilderFields();
            generateDSL();
            connectLiveWebSocket();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>


====================================================================================================
FILE: src/dashboard/server.ts
